PART  IV (B) – LOCAL GOVERNMENT

No. 2308/33 – FRIDAY, DECEMBER  02, 2022
This Gazette Extraordinary can be downloaded from www.documents.gov.lk
1A – PG6071 – 10 (12/2022)
PRADESHIYA  SABHA - ARACHCHIKATTUWA
IT is hereby notiﬁ ed for the public information that it has been adopted under the resolution No. 04/01 moved at the General 
Conference held on 07.04.2022 at Pradeshiya Sabha Arachchikattuwa that all the roads and thoroughfares for which legal action 
had not been ﬁ led in a proper judicial Court before the date speciﬁ ed or roads and thoroughfares conﬁ rmed as the roads and 
thoroughfares that should be owned by Pradeshiya Sabha Arachchikattuwa as per the Decree of a Judicial Court in which a 
case had been ﬁ led before the said date and not mentioned in the following schedule from among the roads and thoroughfares 
tiven in the list of the schedule of the notiﬁ  caiton published in the Extraordinary Gazette No. 2283/04 dated 06.06.2022 
according to the resolution No. 04/01 made at the Pradeshiya Sa bha conference held on 07.04.2022, shall be conﬁ rmed as 
roads and thoroughfares owned by the Pradeshiya Sabha Arachchikattuwa in terms of orders made by the series of “Orders on 
publicaiton of notiﬁ cations speciﬁ ying preparation of plans and lists for roads and thoroughfares maintained by the Pradeshiya 
Sabha within the North Western Province” published by Extraordinary Gazette No. 2238/35 and dated 30.07.2021 by the 
Hon. Governor in the North Western Province and in terms of the  order by Section 24(1) of Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 
of 1987. 
   It is further notiﬁ  ed that a list of said roads and throughfares has been included in the schedule hereto and all the roads 
and throughfares mentioned in that schedule shall be considered as roads and throughfares owned by the Pradeshiya Sabha 
Arachchikattuwa under Sub Section (5) of Section 24 of Pradeshiya Sabha Act.    
 K. Tඁൾർඁർඁൺඇൺආඈඈඋඍඁං,
 Chairman,
 Pradeshiya Sabha, Arachchikattuwa.
At Arachchikattuwa Pradeshiya Sabha, Head Oﬃ  ce,
30th November, 2022.
Resolution 
 Pradeshiya Sabha Arachchikattuwa proposes that the roads and thoroughfares for which legal actions had not been ﬁ led in 
a proper Judicial Court and not mentioned in the following Schedule from among the roads and thoroughfares given in the 
list of the schedule of the notiﬁ cation published in the Extraordinary Gazette No. 2283/04 and dated 06.06.2022 according 
to the resolution No. 04/01 made at the Pradeshiya Sabha confer ence held on 07.04.2022, shall be conﬁ  rmed as roads 
and thoroughfares owned by the Pradeshiya Sabha Arachchikattuwa in terms of orders made by the series of “Orders on 
publication of notiﬁ cations specifying preparation of plans and lists for roads and thoroughfares maintained by the Pradeshiya 
Sabha within the North Western Province” published by Extraordinary Gazette No. 2238/35 and dated 30.07.2021 by the 
Hon. Governor in the North Western Province and in terms of the  order by Section 24(1) of Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 
of 1987.
